        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

### Analysis



<span class="line"><!---->### Analysis<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The attached PoC triggers following ASAN complain if you keep clicking around texts. I believe "ProbeForLowSeverityLifetimeIssue" in the stack trace means an object is deleted, but a dangling pointer is dancing around. Sadly the PoC is unstable and does not show usage of this dangling pointer. The stack trace should give you enough information to fix this issue. If you need to see triggering this issue in action, please let me know and I can provide you with a demo. Please add "hosselot AT



<span class="line"><!---->The attached PoC triggers following ASAN complain if you keep clicking around texts. I believe "ProbeForLowSeverityLifetimeIssue" in the stack trace means an object is deleted, but a dangling pointer is dancing around. Sadly the PoC is unstable and does not show usage of this dangling pointer. The stack trace should give you enough information to fix this issue. If you need to see triggering this issue in action, please let me know and I can provide you with a demo. Please add "hosselot AT<!----></span>

<br>



<br>





-- CVSS -----------------------------------------



<span class="line"><!---->-- CVSS -----------------------------------------<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





4.3: AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:R/S:U/C:L/I:N/A:N



<span class="line"><!---->4.3: AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:R/S:U/C:L/I:N/A:N<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





-- ABSTRACT -------------------------------------



<span class="line"><!---->-- ABSTRACT -------------------------------------<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Trend Micro's Zero Day Initiative has identified a vulnerability affecting the following products:



<span class="line"><!---->Trend Micro's Zero Day Initiative has identified a vulnerability affecting the following products:<!----></span>



<br>





Google - PDFium



<span class="line"><!---->Google - PDFium<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





-- VULNERABILITY DETAILS ------------------------



<span class="line"><!---->-- VULNERABILITY DETAILS ------------------------<!----></span>



<br>

Version tested: 115.0.5773.0 (Developer Build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->Version tested: 115.0.5773.0 (Developer Build) (64-bit)<!----></span>

Platform tested: Windows 10 Enterprise x64 version 22H2 (OS Build 19045.2965)



<span class="line"><!---->Platform tested: Windows 10 Enterprise x64 version 22H2 (OS Build 19045.2965)<!----></span>



<br>





Analysis



<span class="line"><!---->Analysis<!----></span>



<br>





The attached PoC triggers following ASAN complain if you keep clicking around texts. I believe "ProbeForLowSeverityLifetimeIssue" in the stack trace means an object is deleted, but a dangling pointer is dancing around. Sadly the PoC is unstable and does not show usage of this dangling pointer. The stack trace should give you enough information to fix this issue. If you need to see triggering this issue in action, please let me know and I can provide you with a demo. Please add "hosselot AT

Sadly the PoC is unstable and does not show usage of this dangling pointer. The stack trace should give you enough information to fix this issue. If you need to see triggering this issue in action, please let me know and I can provide you with a demo. Please add "hosselot AT<!----></span>

-- INFORMATION ABOUT THE ZDI --------------------



<span class="line"><!---->-- INFORMATION ABOUT THE ZDI --------------------<!----></span>



<br>





Established by TippingPoint and acquired by Trend Micro, the Zero Day Initiative (ZDI) neither re-sells vulnerability details nor exploit code. Instead, upon notifying the affected product vendor, the ZDI provides its Trend Micro TippingPoint customers with zero day protection through its intrusion prevention technology. Explicit details regarding the specifics of the vulnerability are not exposed to any parties until an official vendor patch is publicly available.
